En la última oleada de feminismo argentino se popularizó a niveles insospechados el término “deconstrucción”, creado por el filósofo francés Jacques Derrida. No me importa que los conceptos filosóficos se reciclen hasta volverse irreconocibles, y supongo que tampoco le habría importado a Derrida, que si en algo no creía era en los significados inmutables, pero creo que hay un matiz que sí sería interesante recuperar de la idea de la deconstrucción tal como la planteó él

Strategic Consulting Tools and methods for successful strategy missions (Philippe Chereau, Pierre-Xavier Meschi) (Z-Library)  
- La subrayado en la página 7-7 | Añadido el domingo, 24 de septiembre de 2023 12:08:39

Assessing the Environment 2.1 The Consulting Mission Te environment is a generic term in strategy. It does not have today’s somewhat ecological connotation. In its strategic understanding, the environment refers to an ecosystem where a set of distinct players interact individually and collectively with the company.Tus, all companies operating in a specifc industry are embedded within the associated ecosystem.
==========
Strategic Consulting Tools and methods for successful strategy missions (Philippe Chereau, Pierre-Xavier Meschi) (Z-Library)  
- La subrayado en la página 8-8 | Añadido el domingo, 24 de septiembre de 2023 12:15:47

Tis assessment of the environment is one of the most classic missions for a consulting frm.However, the consultant should not lose sight of the fact that the conclusions of this mission are crucial for the client company.Indeed, the environment’s value and attractiveness directly impact the company’s growth and proftability.
==========
Strategic Consulting Tools and methods for successful strategy missions (Philippe Chereau, Pierre-Xavier Meschi) (Z-Library)  
- La subrayado en la página 8-8 | Añadido el domingo, 24 de septiembre de 2023 12:18:17

A frst series of consulting missions consists of helping CEOs and top managers clarify the boundaries and challenges of their company’s current or future environment. Tis involves updating their data and formalising their observations and intuitions related to assessing the value of the company’s environment. Tese missions are often linked to an internal analysis of the company’s competences and resources (human, technological, fnancial…). For the company seeking to achieve strategic ft, this internal analysis has to be aligned with the external analysis of the environment’s opportunities and threats. On this basis, the consultant can check whether the client company is able to respond to the environment’s opportunities and threats and thus build a solid competitive advantage.
==========
Strategic Consulting Tools and methods for successful strategy missions (Philippe Chereau, Pierre-Xavier Meschi) (Z-Library)  
- La subrayado en la página 8-8 | Añadido el domingo, 24 de septiembre de 2023 12:19:44

- La subrayado en la página 9-9 | Añadido el domingo, 24 de septiembre de 2023 12:21:01

A second series of missions seeks (i) to identify and evaluate the key players of an environment (in terms of threat, competences and resources, proftability and value capture), (ii) to monitor the behaviour and strategy of these key players, and (iii) to suggest strategic responses and scenarios, including direct competition or collaboration with these players.Here, the key questions asked by CEOs and top managers are
==========

- La subrayado en la página 9-9 | Añadido el domingo, 24 de septiembre de 2023 12:22:28

A third series of missions occurs when the company intends to grow into new geographical markets, new client segments and/or new businesses. Te assessment of the associated environment is necessary before any decision to expand is made
==========
Strategic Consulting Tools and methods for successful strategy missions (Philippe Chereau, Pierre-Xavier Meschi) (Z-Library)  
- La subrayado en la página 9-9 | Añadido el domingo, 24 de septiembre de 2023 12:25:39

- La subrayado en la página 10-10 | Añadido el domingo, 24 de septiembre de 2023 12:28:38

A ffth and fnal series of missions relates to business refocusing and divestment decisions. For a diversifed company, regular assessment of the environment (of each geographical market, product/client segment and business) allows a review of the company’s diﬀerent (products, activities, competences, alliances…) portfolios and to restructure them if needed

Theory, Methodology and the Tools for the Mission 2.2.1 Theoretical Background Missions aiming to assess the environment are based on solid theoretical frameworks that have empirically proved their added value. Most come from industrial economics. Tese consulting missions are based on the assumption that the value and attractiveness of the company’s environment determine its proftability and survival. Tis theory was initially postulated by Joe S.Bain, professor of economics at Berkeley, in his Industrial Organization, published in 1959. In 1970, Frederic M.Scherer, professor of economics at Harvard’s Kennedy School of Government, took Bain’s research further in Industrial

Most come from industrial economics. Tese consulting missions are based on the assumption that the value and attractiveness of the company’s environment determine its proftability and survival.

Scherer advocates structuring the relationship between the company’s environment and its performance using the “SCP” (“Structure-Conduct-Performance”) paradigm
==========
Strategic Consulting Tools and methods for successful strategy missions (Philippe Chereau, Pierre-Xavier Meschi) (Z-Library)  
- La subrayado en la página 11-11 | Añadido el domingo, 24 de septiembre de 2023 12:37:27

Scherer shows that the market structure, the behaviour of companies operating in this market and their performance follow a causal sequence
==========
Strategic Consulting Tools and methods for successful strategy missions (Philippe Chereau, Pierre-Xavier Meschi) (Z-Library)  
- La subrayado en la página 11-11 | Añadido el domingo, 24 de septiembre de 2023 12:42:17

Te SCP paradigm benefted from a major advance thanks to the research of Michael E.Porter, professor of strategy at Harvard Business School
==========
Strategic Consulting Tools and methods for successful strategy missions (Philippe Chereau, Pierre-Xavier Meschi) (Z-Library)  
- La subrayado en la página 11-11 | Añadido el domingo, 24 de septiembre de 2023 12:44:45

Porter proposed assessing the structure and value of a market from a model that combined not just one (competition), but a whole set of competitive forces. A thorough assessment of a market structure requires the inclusion of other players adjacent to the competition: suppliers, clients, new entrants and substitutes. In fact, within Porter’s model, the intensity of competition is only one competitive force among others, and it is this inﬂuence combined with other competitive forces that determines successively the value and attractiveness of an environment, the strategy of companies and their performance.
==========
Strategic Consulting Tools and methods for successful strategy missions (Philippe Chereau, Pierre-Xavier Meschi) (Z-Library)

By teaching his model to multiple cohorts of MBA students at Harvard Business School in the 1980s and 1990s, Porter largely contributed to the dissemination of the SCP paradigm within SMEs, multinationals and large strategy consulting frms. 3 By isolating the opportunities and threats resulting from the evaluation of competitive forces, he also complemented one of the frst tools for strategic analysis, the “SWOT” (“Strengths, Weaknesses, Opportunities, Treats”) method, which has been in use since the 1970s.
==========
Strategic Consulting Tools and methods for successful strategy missions (Philippe Chereau, Pierre-Xavier Meschi) (Z-Library)  
- La subrayado en la página 14-14 | Añadido el domingo, 24 de septiembre de 2023 12:54:31

Methodology and Tools for the Mission Te strategy literature abounds in tools for strategic analysis, namely, tools intended to assess the value and attractiveness of an environment. Strategic analysis is by far the dimension of strategy that has produced the most tools for consultants.However, when a consultant is hired by a company to assess its environment, he/she may wonder not so much which tool to use but rather which methodology to deploy.Indeed, a methodology suited to this kind of mission should propose a few tools in a step-by-step approach. Each step corresponds to a specifc tool and each tool produces information, analyses and knowledge, which should allow the consultant to obtain the most refned and thorough assessment of the environment while remaining coherent with the client company’s frame of reference.
==========

Quadrant 2 – not urgent but important
==========

- La subrayado en la posición 223-227 | Añadido el martes, 26 de septiembre de 2023 00:57:52

Tasks that don’t have a high urgency, but play an important role in the future. This is where you do your strategic planning, and anything related to education, health, recreation, exercise, and/career. The tasks in here might not be urgent in the present, but in the long term this quadrant is where you might want to spend most of your time. The more time you spend here, the less time you’ll have to spend in Quadrant 1 where the stress happens . The better your planning is in Quadrant 2, the less future tasks will be found in quadrant 1.

Here is a guide to some of the latest trends in digital marketing, many of which we cover in more detail later in this book. Personalization Personalization has become increasingly important in digital marketing as consumers expect a more personalized experience. The buyers would quickly say that the new option was not right for them and then more often than not choose in favor of the one it was dominated by. Why? As detrimental as the status quo bias is to influence, there is one proven way to use it in your favor: change the default option. Normally, buyers are given a choice to opt in to something, but what if you change this choice and instead let them opt out? WHY #4: WHY YOU AND YOUR COMPANY?
==========
The Science of Selling  David Hoffeld Proven Strategies to Make Your Pitch, Influence Decisions, and Close the Deal (David Hoffeld) (Z-Library) (David Hoffeld)
- La subrayado en la página 64 | posición 1160-1163 | Añadido el jueves, 18 de julio de 2024 23:35:27

there is “an asymmetry in available information” between buyers and sellers.13 The core of what he meant was that though sellers know the true nature of their products or services, potential customers will not find it out until after purchasing it, which escalates the risk associated with making a purchase.
==========
The Science of Selling  David Hoffeld Proven Strategies to Make Your Pitch, Influence Decisions, and Close the Deal (David Hoffeld) (Z-Library) (David Hoffeld)
- La subrayado en la página 64 | posición 1163-1164 | Añadido el jueves, 18 de julio de 2024 23:35:34

His research also revealed that the best way to reduce a buyer’s perception of risk is through trust.
==========
The Science of Selling  David Hoffeld Proven Strategies to Make Your Pitch, Influence Decisions, and Close the Deal (David Hoffeld) (Z-Library) (David Hoffeld)
- La subrayado en la página 64 | posición 1164-1167 | Añadido el jueves, 18 de julio de 2024 23:35:44

The more a buyer trusts you and the company you represent, the more receptive they will be and the less risk they will associate with acquiring your product or service.14 That is what trust does: it makes a decision feel safe. The opposite is also true. Without trust, a buying decision will feel hazardous.

Superficiales -  Qué está haciendo In... (Z-Library) (Nicholas Carr)
- La subrayado en la página 49 | posición 637-643 | Añadido el sábado, 23 de noviembre de 2024 14:24:11

A continuación los participantes se dividieron en dos grupos. Pidió a los miembros de uno de los grupos que practicaran la melodía en un piano dos horas al día durante los próximos cinco. Luego pidió a los miembros del otro grupo que se sentaran delante del piano durante la misma cantidad de tiempo, pero que se limitaran a imaginar que tocaban la melodía, sin llegar siquiera a tocar las teclas. Mediante una técnica llamada estimulación magnética transcraneal, o TMS, Pascual-Leone registró la actividad cerebral de todos los participantes antes, durante y después de la prueba. Encontró que la gente que solo había imaginado tocar las notas presentaba exactamente los mismos cambios en su cerebro que los que de hecho las habían tocado al piano[50]. Su cerebro había cambiado en respuesta

Enfócate en lo que deseas de verdad, usa tu pasión para ilusionarte en un proyecto grande —¡o pequeño!— pero que despierte lo más profundo de tu ser, y comenzarás a sentir que algo sucede en tu interior. Ganas en seguridad, en confianza, en alegría… Y, algo más sorprendente aún, tu cerebro cambia. Estados de ilusión mantenidos a lo largo de unos días activan un proceso de neurogénesis: células madre acuden al hipocampo —zona de memoria y aprendizaje— y se transforman en neuronas. Conocemos pocas maneras de regenerar nuevas células neuronales, ¡la pasión y la ilusión son una de ellas!
